  import { ThemeSwitcher } from '/docs/js/modules/theme-switcher.js';

  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
    const themeSwitchers = document.querySelectorAll('[data-theme-toggle]');

</script> <div class="content-group"> <main id="site-main"> <nav class="site-breadcrumbs" aria-label="Breadcrumb"> <ol vocab="http://schema.org/" typeof="BreadcrumbList"> <li property="itemListElement" typeof="ListItem"> <meta property="position" content="0"> <a property="item" typeof="WebPage" href="/docs" aria-current="page"> <span property="name">Docs</span> </a> </li>  </ol> </nav> <article itemscope itemtype="https://schema.org/Article"> <header class="header">  <div class="header__text"> <h1 class="header__title">Hello, Octopus Deploy! ð</h1> <p class="header__subtitle">Best-of-breed Continuous Delivery</p> </div> </header> <div class="page-content anim-show-parent" itemprop="articleBody"> <p>Octopus Deploy is a sophisticated, best-of-breed continuous delivery (CD) platform for modern software teams. Octopus offers powerful release orchestration, deployment automation, and runbook automation, while handling the scale, complexity and governance expectations of even the largest organizations with the most complex deployment challenges.</p>
<figure><p><img src="/docs/img/getting-started/dashboard.png" alt="Octopus Dashboard"/></p></figure>
<p>Octopus has a modern, friendly user experience that makes it easy for your teams to self-service application releases, and democratizes how you deliver software. Octopus also has a comprehensive API - anything the UI can do, the API can do too.</p>
<p>Octopus takes over where your CI server ends, modelling the entire release orchestration process of software. This includes:</p>
<ul>
<li>Release versioning</li>
<li>Environment promotion (beyond simple dev/test/prod workflows)</li>
<li>Deployment automation</li>
<li>Progressive software delivery (rolling deployments, blue/green, canary)</li>
<li>Configuration management</li>
<li>Approvals &amp; ITSM integration</li>
<li>Deployment freezes</li>
<li>Coordinating deployments across projects and their dependencies</li>
</ul>
<p>You can use Octopus to deploy anything, anywhere. Whether itâs <strong>Kubernetes</strong>, <strong>Linux</strong> or <strong>Windows</strong> virtual machines, <strong>Amazon Web Services</strong>, <strong>Azure</strong>, or <strong>Google Cloud</strong>, so long as Octopus can speak to it via our Tentacle agent, SSH, command line, or a web service, Octopus can deploy to it.</p>
<p>Advanced role-based access control ensures only the right people can deploy to production, all changes are audited, and teams can get their work done without proliferation of admin access to cloud accounts or privileged systems.</p>
<p>Octopus can be self-managed and hosted in your own infrastructure or private cloud, or we can host it for you in Octopus Cloud.</p>
<p>Octopus models deployments in advanced ways that allows you to tame complexity at scale. For example, if âdeploying to productionâ means a coordinated rollout of applications and dependencies across geographically distributed clusters in the cloud on behalf of thousands of end-customers, each with their own instances of your application, or pushing releases out to edge networks or servers running in physical retail stores, hospitals or hotels, Octopus enables you to model this in ways no other CD tool can using <strong>tenanted deployments</strong>.</p>
<p>Built by experienced DevOps practitioners over a decade, and battle tested by thousands of organizations ranging from small teams to large Fortune 100 organizations with tens of thousands of engineers, projects and deployment targets, Octopus embodies a set of principles about what weâve learned in doing CD well:</p>
<ul>
<li>CI is not CD</li>
<li>Build your binaries/containers once</li>
<li>Consistency across processes, teams and environments</li>
<li>Pragmatic use of version control and GitOps</li>
</ul>
<h2 id="why-do-i-need-octopus-i-have-a-cicd-tool">Why do I need Octopus, I have a CI/CD tool</h2>
<p>On most teams, continuous integration (CI) or build automation is a solved problem. Great options like GitHub Actions, GitLab CI, Jenkins, TeamCity, BuildKite, and Azure DevOps exist and are widely used by teams today.</p>
<p>These systems are all designed in a similar way - they monitor source code repositories for changes, compile code, run unit tests, and give software developers fast feedback on their code changes.</p>
<p>For most of these systems, the CD functionality often just means they provide some ability to call a deployment script that you provide - the deployment script is up to you. They might also provide some way to model simple dev/test/production promotion workflows by calling a different deployment script for each environment.</p>
<p>When a software team is starting out, this âput your deployment script hereâ approach to CD can work - the deployment script starts simple. Over time as applications evolve, complexity grows. That âdeployment scriptâ becomes hundreds and thousands of lines of specialized scripts and YAML that at best only a couple of people on the team understand or are comfortable changing. Multiply that over many teams and applications at the company and âDIY shadow CDâ is born. Teams of engineers become dedicated to building custom CD glue to bridge the gap between âput your deployment script hereâ and the realities of the complexity of delivering software at scale.</p>
<figure><p><img src="/docs/img/getting-started/overview.png" alt="Octopus Dashboard"/></p></figure>
<p>Decoupling the CI platform from the CD platform allows teams to bring their favorite CI tool - and most organizations have more than one - while we focus on giving you the most powerful best-of-breed CD capabilities. Octopus integrates with popular CI tools like GitHub Actions, Jenkins or TeamCity, letting them do what they do best - the CI part of the feedback loop. Octopus then takes over âartifact-forwardâ, and handles the release and deployment aspects of CD in advanced ways that no CI/CD tool can.</p>
<p>We promise that when using Octopus, compared to a generic CI/CD tool, youâll spend 1/10th the amount of time building DIY shadow CD glue, and more time shipping new features and delivering valuable software to production.</p>
<h2 id="getting-started">Getting Started</h2>
<p>Octopus is easy to get started with - you can go from zero to fully automating your deployments in minutes.</p>
<p>For a tour of the key Octopus concepts, begin with our <a href="/docs/getting-started">Getting Started</a> guide.</p>
<p>If you deliver software to Kubernetes, our <a href="/docs/deployments/kubernetes">Kubernetes overview</a> is a good starting point.</p>
<p>If you enjoy learning via video, the Octopus 101 recording below also serves as a great introduction to the key Octopus concepts in the context of modern deployments.</p>
<p><a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=y5wP_H_1VqY">Watch the Octopus 101</a></p>
<h2 id="were-here-to-help">Weâre here to help</h2>
<p>We designed Octopus to be easy to learn, but CD is an inherently complex problem domain.</p>
<p>Our 270+ people all over the globe have deep experience in all things CD, and weâre happy to help even when the problem is outside of Octopus.</p>
<p>If you get stuck or just need advice, weâre here to help.</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="mailto:support@octopus.com">Email our support</a> (we typically respond in under 1 hour)</li>
<li><a href="https://octopus.com/slack">Join our community Slack</a></li>
</ul>
<p>Happy deployments!</p>

class="footer__column-title" id="footer-second-sign-up-to-our-newsletter" itemprop="name">
Sign-up to our newsletter
</h3> <ul class="footer__items" aria-labelledby="footer-second-sign-up-to-our-newsletter"> <li class="footer__item footer__item--component"> <div class="mktoFormWrapper"> <form id="mktoForm_2139" class="newsletter__form"></form> <script>(function(){const formId = 2139;
const dreamdataTrackingId = "Newsletter Signup (Footer)";

  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    // @ts-ignore - don't have a global type for MktoForms2
    if (typeof MktoForms2 !== 'undefined' && MktoForms2.loadForm) {
      // @ts-ignore
      MktoForms2.loadForm(
        '//get.octopus.com',
        '271-BEX-827',
        formId,
        (form) => {
          const formElem = form.getFormElem()[0];

          if (formElem instanceof HTMLElement) {
            const styles = formElem.querySelectorAll('style');
            styles.forEach((style) => style.remove());

            const baseStyle = document.getElementById('mktoForms2BaseStyle');
            if (baseStyle) {
              baseStyle.remove();
            }

            formElem.removeAttribute('style');

            formElem
              .querySelectorAll('.mktoTextField')
              .forEach((el) => el.classList.add('form-control'));
            formElem
              .querySelectorAll('.mktoEmailField')
              .forEach((el) => el.classList.add('form-control'));
            formElem
              .querySelectorAll('.mktoButton')
              .forEach((el) => el.classList.add('button', 'button--primary'));

            formElem
              .querySelectorAll('.mktoAsterix')
              .forEach((el) => el.remove());
            formElem
              .querySelectorAll('.mktoOffset')
              .forEach((el) => el.remove());

            formElem.querySelectorAll('.mktoFormCol').forEach((el) => {
              el.removeAttribute('style');
            });

            formElem.querySelectorAll('.mktoField').forEach((el) => {
              el.removeAttribute('style');
            });

            formElem.querySelectorAll('.mktoLabel').forEach((el) => {
              el.removeAttribute('style');
            });

            // Add Dreamdata tracking if configured
            if (dreamdataTrackingId) {
              form.onSuccess(function (values, followUpUrl) {
                const email = values.Email || values.email;

                // Track with Dreamdata if available
                if (typeof dreamdata !== 'undefined') {
                  try {
                    dreamdata.track(dreamdataTrackingId);
                    if (email) {
                      dreamdata.identify(null, {
                        email: email,
                      });
                    }
                  } catch (error) {
                    console.warn('Dreamdata tracking failed:', error);
                  }
                } else {
                  console.warn(
                    'Dreamdata not available for tracking:',
                    dreamdataTrackingId
                  );
                }

                // Continue with normal form submission flow
                if (followUpUrl) {
                  location.href = followUpUrl;
                }

                // Return false to prevent default redirect
                return followUpUrl ? false : true;
              });
            }
          } else {
            console.error(
              'Expected a DOM element but got something else',
              formElem
            );
          }
        }
      );
    } else {
      console.error(
        'MktoForms2 is not available. Check if the script is correctly loaded.'
      );
    }
  });
})();</script> </div> </li> </ul> </div> <div class="footer__column"> <h3 class="footer__column-title" id="footer-second-marketplaces" itemprop="name">
